**assistant:** Now I have a complete picture of available records for Licking County, Ohio. Let me write the plan.

**Survey findings:**
- **1820–1840 censuses**: Available on FamilySearch (heads-of-household only; children by age/sex tally — Peter would appear through 1836, Rebecca as head from 1840)
- **1850–1870 censuses**: Fully indexed, name all household members — Rebecca appears in these
- **Probate**: Ohio Probate Records, 1789–1996 (collection 1992421) covers Licking Co.; also fulltext-searchable partition records 1816–1844 (court land-heir proceedings)
- **County marriage records**: Indexed 1808–2016 (collection 1614804); Licking Co. marriage index 1808–1879 also available
- **Parish records**: Granville Township 1831–1848 (browse-only); Presbyterian records for Newark, Utica, Pataskala (browse-only)
- **County death records**: Collection 2128172, indexed
- **Tax records**: Multiple indexed volumes for 1816–1840 (Peter already appears in tree for 1823–1834)
- **NOTE**: A "Transcribed Burnt Record" (1867–1872 probate) signals a courthouse fire, but records from 1836 should predate it
